(NYSE:NKE) today reported fiscal 2020 financial results for its </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">November&#160;30, 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Revenue increased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$10.3 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">10 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a reported basis and up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">13 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a currency-neutral basis*, driven by strong growth across all geographies.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;In Q2, NIKE has proven again that innovation is our greatest competitive edge </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8212;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;turning athlete insights into breakthrough product and digital services, as we offer more choice to more consumers at an accelerated pace,&#8221; said Mark Parker, Chairman, President and CEO, NIKE, Inc. &#8220;Our entire NIKE team is fueling our current momentum, and I&#8217;ve never been more optimistic about the future of this company.&#8221;**</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Diluted earnings per share for the quarter was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.70</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">35</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent driven primarily by strong revenue growth, gross margin expansion, selling and administrative expense leverage, a lower tax rate and a lower average share count.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;NIKE delivered another strong quarter of accelerating, high-quality growth, driven by strategic and targeted investment in our digital transformation,&#8221; said Andy Campion, Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer, NIKE, Inc. &#8220;As we deliver a relentless flow of innovation and scale NIKE&#8217;s digital advantage, we are positioned for even greater competitive separation and long-term shareholder value creation.&#8221;**</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Income Statement Review</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; Direct and global operations. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td As of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">November&#160;30, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a total of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">33.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;shares had been repurchased under this program for approximately </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.9 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">NIKE, Inc. management will host a conference call beginning at approximately 2:00 p.m. PT on December 19, 2019, to review fiscal second quarter results. The conference call will be broadcast live via the Internet and can be accessed at http://investors.nike.com. For those unable to listen to the live broadcast, an archived version will be available at the same location through 9:00 p.m. PT, January 9, 2020. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">About NIKE, Inc.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">NIKE, Inc., based near Beaverton, Oregon, is the world's leading designer, marketer and distributor of authentic athletic footwear, apparel, equipment and accessories for a wide variety of sports and fitness activities. Converse, a wholly-owned NIKE, Inc. subsidiary brand, designs, markets and distributes athletic lifestyle footwear, apparel and accessories.
